190: <script>
191:         function togglePassword() {
192:             const pwInput = document.getElementById('password');
193:             const pwIcon = document.getElementById('pw-icon');
194:             
195:             if (pwInput.type === 'password') {
196:                 pwInput.type = 'text';
197:                 pwIcon.textContent = 'visibility_off';
198:             } else {
199:                 pwInput.type = 'password';
200:                 pwIcon.textContent = 'visibility';
201:             }
202:         }
203: 
204:         // Add subtle focus ring effect to the card on interaction
205:         const formInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input');
206:         const loginCard = document.querySelector('.custom-shadow');
207:         
208:         formInputs.forEach(input => {
209:             input.addEventListener('focus', () => {
210:                 loginCard.style.boxShadow = '0 10px 25px -5px rgba(0, 91, 191, 0.1), 0 8px 10px -6px rgba(0, 91, 191, 0.1)';
211:             });
212:             input.addEventListener('blur', () => {
213:                 loginCard.style.boxShadow = '0 2px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08)';
214:             });
215:         });
216:     </script>

109: 
110: ## Brand & Style
111: 
112: The design system is engineered for a high-performance Learning Management System (LMS) specifically tailored for SMA/SMK environments. The brand personality is **Professional, Systematic, and Trustworthy**, prioritizing clarity and ease of navigation for three distinct user archetypes: Admins, Teachers, and Students.
113: 
114: The visual style is **Corporate Modern**, characterized by:
115: - **High Information Density:** Clean layouts that allow for complex data (grades, schedules, curricula) to be scanned quickly.
116: - **Structural Integrity:** Use of rigid alignment and consistent spacing to evoke a sense of institutional reliability.
117: - **Minimalist Aesthetic:** Stripping away decorative elements like gradients or complex illustrations to focus purely on educational content.
118: - **Functional Clarity:** Ensuring that the UI feels mature and sophisticated, intentionally avoiding "gamified" or "childish" tropes often found in primary education software.
119: 
120: ## Colors
121: 
122: The palette is anchored by a high-trust **Primary Blue**, used specifically for actionable items and brand identifiers. 
123: 
124: - **Primary (#1A73E8):** Used for primary buttons, active states, and focus indicators.
125: - **Neutral Surface (#F5F6FA):** Applied to card backgrounds, sidebars, and secondary layout containers to create subtle separation from the white page background.
126: - **Typography Primary (#202124):** High-contrast dark gray for maximum legibility in body text and headings.
127: - **Typography Secondary (#5F6368):** Medium gray for labels, hints, and meta-data.
128: - **Semantic Colors:** Green and Red are reserved for grading status, submission success, or error alerts, following the standard professional utility scale.
129: 
130: ## Typography
131: 
132: This design system utilizes **Inter** as the sole typeface family to ensure a clean, systematic feel across all platforms. The scale is built on a 14px base for standard body content, optimized for data-heavy portals.
133: 
134: - **Headlines:** Use semi-bold weights with slight negative letter-spacing to appear compact and authoritative.
135: - **Body Text:** Standardized at 14px (`body-md`) for dashboards and 16px (`body-lg`) for long-form reading materials or lesson content.
136: - **Labels:** Used for table headers, small captions, and tag text. These are slightly tighter and use a medium weight for clarity.
137: - **Monospaced:** JetBrains Mono is suggested for any technical SMK subjects involving programming or technical data.
138: 
139: ## Layout & Spacing
140: 
141: The layout follows a **Fixed Grid** philosophy for desktop dashboards to ensure consistent information density, while transitioning to a **Fluid Grid** for mobile views.
142: 
143: - **The 8px Grid:** All internal spacing (padding, margins between elements) must be multiples of 4px/8px to maintain mathematical harmony.
144: - **Desktop:** 12-column grid with 24px gutters. The main navigation sidebar is fixed at 256px, while the content area expands to a maximum of 1440px.
145: - **Tablet:** 8-column grid with 20px gutters. Sidebars usually collapse into a hamburger menu or narrow icon bar.
146: - **Mobile:** 4-column fluid grid with 16px outer margins. Vertical stacking is mandatory for all card-based content.
147: 
148: ## Elevation & Depth
149: 
150: To maintain a professional and flat aesthetic, depth is communicated through **Tonal Layers** and a single, disciplined shadow style.
151: 
152: - **Base Layer:** The white (#FFFFFF) background represents the lowest level.
153: - **Surface Layer:** The light gray (#F5F6FA) is used for "Well" areas or section containers that house multiple cards.
154: - **Card Elevation:** High-priority content containers use a white background with a specific "Soft Shadow": `0 2px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08)`. This provides just enough lift to separate content without appearing heavy.
155: - **Interactive States:** On hover, cards may increase shadow spread slightly (`0 4px 12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12)`) to indicate clickability.
156: - **Borders:** 1px solid borders in #E0E0E0 are used for input fields and table rows instead of shadows to keep the UI crisp.
157: 
158: ## Shapes
159: 
160: The design system utilizes **Soft** roundedness to balance professional rigor with modern approachability.
161: 
162: - **Standard Elements (0.25rem / 4px):** Applied to buttons, input fields, and small tags. This "sharp-soft" look maintains a serious, academic tone.
163: - **Large Elements (0.5rem / 8px):** Applied to cards, modals, and featured image containers.
164: - **Full Rounded:** Only used for "Pill" tags (e.g., status indicators like "Completed" or "Pending") and user avatars.
165: 
166: ## Components
167: 
168: - **Buttons:** Primary buttons use the Primary Blue with white text. Secondary buttons use a transparent background with a #E0E0E0 border and #202124 text. No gradients allowed.
169: - **Input Fields:** 1px solid border (#E0E0E0). On focus, the border changes to Primary Blue with a 2px thickness. Labels are always visible above the field in `label-sm`.
170: - **Cards:** White background, 8px corner radius, and the standard 0 2px 8px shadow. Used for course modules, student profiles, and grade reports.
171: - **Chips/Status:** Small height (24px or 32px), pill-shaped. Background colors should be very desaturated (e.g., light green for "Passed") with high-contrast dark text.
172: - **Lists/Tables:** Use alternating row colors (White and #F5F6FA) or simple 1px dividers. Table headers must be in `label-sm` with a light gray background.
173: - **Navigation:** Vertical sidebar for desktop with icons (24px) paired with `body-md` text. Active state indicated by a 4px vertical bar on the left edge in Primary Blue.
174: - **LMS Specifics:**
175:     - *Grade Indicator:* A dedicated circular or box-shaped badge with a bold weight for the score.
176:     - *Timeline/Progress Bar:* A simple 4px thick horizontal track using #F5F6FA with a Primary Blue fill indicating completion percentage.

(End of file - total 176 lines)

390:         tabButtons.forEach(btn => {
391:             btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
392:                 tabButtons.forEach(b => {
393:                     b.classList.remove('bg-primary-container', 'text-on-primary-container', 'font-bold');
394:                     b.classList.add('text-on-surface-variant');
395:                     const icon = b.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined');
396:                     if(icon) icon.remove();
397:                 });
398:                 btn.classList.add('bg-primary-container', 'text-on-primary-container', 'font-bold');
399:                 btn.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant');
400:                 const span = document.createElement('span');
401:                 span.className = 'material-symbols-outlined text-[18px]';
402:                 span.style.fontVariationSettings = "'FILL' 1";
403:                 span.textContent = 'check_circle';
404:                 btn.appendChild(span);
405:             });
406:         });

399:         const fileInput = document.querySelector('input[type="file"]');
400: 
401:         dropZone.addEventListener('click', () => fileInput.click());
402: 
403:         dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
404:             e.preventDefault();
405:             dropZone.classList.add('border-primary', 'bg-primary-container/10');
406:         });
407: 
408:         dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
409:             dropZone.classList.remove('border-primary', 'bg-primary-container/10');
410:         });
411: 
412:         dropZone.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
413:             e.preventDefault();
414:             dropZone.classList.remove('border-primary', 'bg-primary-container/10');
415:             const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
416:             if (files.length > 0) {
417:                 alert(`${files.length} file(s) siap diunggah.`);
418:             }
419:         });
420: 
421:         // Simpan Materi Button Animation
422:         const saveBtn = document.querySelector('button.bg-primary');

426:                 this.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined text-[18px]">check_circle</span> Berhasil';

372: <script>
373:         // Micro-interactions for accessibility and flair
374:         document.querySelectorAll('tr').forEach(row => {
375:             row.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
376:                 row.classList.add('bg-surface-container-lowest');
377:             });
378:             row.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
379:                 row.classList.remove('bg-surface-container-lowest');
380:             });
381:         });
382: 
383:         // Simple observer for chart animation
384:         const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
385:             entries.forEach(entry => {
386:                 if (entry.isIntersecting) {
387:                     entry.target.classList.add('opacity-100');
388:                 }
389:             });
390:         });
391: 
392:         document.querySelectorAll('.flex-1.flex.flex-col').forEach(bar => {
393:             observer.observe(bar);

373:                 setTimeout(() => btn.classList.remove('scale-95'), 150);
374:             });
375:         });
376: 
377:         // Search Input atmospheric effect
378:         const searchInput = document.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
379:         searchInput.addEventListener('focus', () => {
380:             searchInput.parentElement.classList.add('ring-2', 'ring-primary/20');
381:         });
382:         searchInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
383:             searchInput.parentElement.classList.remove('ring-2', 'ring-primary/20');
384:         });
385:     </script>
386: </body></html>

(End of file - total 386 lines)
</content>
```

### In Progress

- (none)

## Key Decisions

48: └── sql/
49:     └── simp_web.sql                 # File dump database
50: ```
51: 
52: ---
53: 
54: ## BAGIAN 2 : SKEMA DATABASE LENGKAP (MySQL)
55: 
56: ```sql
57: -- --------------------------------------------------------
58: -- Database: simp_web
59: -- --------------------------------------------------------
60: 
61: CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS simp_web CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
62: USE simp_web;
63: 
64: -- Tabel: users
65: CREATE TABLE users (
66:     id          INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
67:     nama        VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
68:     email       VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
69:     password    VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,           -- bcrypt hash
70:     role        ENUM('admin','guru','siswa') NOT NULL,
71:     created_at  TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
72: );
73: 
74: -- Tabel: kelas
75: CREATE TABLE kelas (
76:     id_kelas    INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
77:     nama_kelas  VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
78:     wali_kelas  INT,                             -- FK -> users.id (role guru)
79:     FOREIGN KEY (wali_kelas) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL
80: );
81: 
82: -- Tabel: kelas_siswa (relasi many-to-many siswa & kelas)
83: CREATE TABLE kelas_siswa (
84:     id          INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
85:     id_kelas    INT NOT NULL,
86:     id_siswa    INT NOT NULL,
87:     FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE,
88:     FOREIGN KEY (id_siswa) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
89: );
90: 
91: -- Tabel: materi
92: CREATE TABLE materi (
93:     id_materi       INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
94:     id_guru         INT NOT NULL,
95:     id_kelas        INT NOT NULL,
96:     judul           VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
97:     deskripsi       TEXT,
98:     file            VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,        -- path file upload
99:     tanggal_upload  DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
100:     FOREIGN KEY (id_guru)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
101:     FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE
102: );
103: 
104: -- Tabel: tugas
105: CREATE TABLE tugas (
106:     id_tugas    INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
107:     id_guru     INT NOT NULL,
108:     id_kelas    INT NOT NULL,
109:     judul       VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
110:     deskripsi   TEXT,
111:     deadline    DATETIME NOT NULL,
112:     created_at  TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
113:     FOREIGN KEY (id_guru)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
114:     FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE
115: );
116: 
117: -- Tabel: pengumpulan_tugas
118: CREATE TABLE pengumpulan_tugas (
119:     id_pengumpulan  INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
120:     id_tugas        INT NOT NULL,
121:     id_siswa        INT NOT NULL,
122:     file            VARCHAR(255),                 -- path file jawaban
123:     nilai           FLOAT DEFAULT NULL,
124:     status          ENUM('belum','dikumpulkan','dinilai') DEFAULT 'belum',
125:     waktu_kumpul    DATETIME,
126:     FOREIGN KEY (id_tugas)  REFERENCES tugas(id_tugas) ON DELETE CASCADE,
127:     FOREIGN KEY (id_siswa)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
128: );
129: 
130: -- Tabel: absensi (sesi per kelas per tanggal)
131: CREATE TABLE absensi (
132:     id_absensi  INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
133:     id_kelas    INT NOT NULL,
134:     id_guru     INT NOT NULL,
135:     tanggal     DATE NOT NULL,
136:     FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE,
137:     FOREIGN KEY (id_guru)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
138: );
139: 
140: -- Tabel: absensi_detail (status kehadiran tiap siswa)
141: CREATE TABLE absensi_detail (
142:     id_detail   INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
143:     id_absensi  INT NOT NULL,
144:     id_siswa    INT NOT NULL,
145:     status      ENUM('hadir','izin','sakit','alfa') DEFAULT 'alfa',
146:     FOREIGN KEY (id_absensi) REFERENCES absensi(id_absensi) ON DELETE CASCADE,
147:     FOREIGN KEY (id_siswa)   REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
148: );
149: ```
150:

152: 
153: ## BAGIAN 3 : DESKRIPSI HALAMAN & FITUR PER ROLE
154: 
155: ### [A] HALAMAN PUBLIK
156: 
157: #### 1. Halaman Login (login.php)
158: 
159: | Elemen | Deskripsi |
160: |--------|-----------|
161: | Form | email, password |
162: | Validasi | cek ke tabel users |
163: | Jika valid | set session (id, nama, role), redirect ke dashboard sesuai role |
164: | Jika tidak valid | tampilkan pesan error |
165: | Session keys | `$_SESSION['user_id']`, `$_SESSION['nama']`, `$_SESSION['role']` |
166: 
167: ### [B] ADMIN
168: 
169: #### 1. Dashboard Admin
170: 
171: - Ringkasan statistik: total guru, total siswa, total kelas
172: - Aktivitas terbaru (log tugas / materi terbaru)
173: 
174: #### 2. Kelola Kelas
175: 
176: - Tampilkan daftar kelas (tabel: nama_kelas, wali_kelas)
177: - Tombol: Tambah Kelas, Edit, Hapus
178: - Form Tambah/Edit: nama_kelas, pilih wali_kelas (dropdown guru)
179: - Assign siswa ke kelas (checkbox list siswa)
180: 
181: #### 3. Kelola Akun Pengguna
182: 
183: - Tab: Guru | Siswa
184: - Tampilkan daftar sesuai role
185: - Tombol: Tambah, Edit, Hapus
186: - Form: nama, email, password (auto-hash bcrypt), role
187: - Reset password opsional saat edit
188: 
189: #### 4. Laporan
190: 
191: - Filter: pilih kelas, pilih periode (bulan/semester)
192: - Tampilkan rekap nilai per siswa per kelas
193: - Tampilkan rekap absensi per siswa per kelas
194: - Tombol: Export ke PDF / Print
195: 
196: ### [C] GURU
197: 
198: #### 1. Dashboard Guru
199: 
200: - Menu cepat: Upload Materi, Buat Tugas, Absensi, Nilai, Laporan
201: - Daftar tugas aktif yang belum melewati deadline
202: - Notifikasi tugas yang sudah dikumpulkan siswa (belum dinilai)
203: 
204: #### 2. Upload Materi
205: 
206: - Form: judul, deskripsi, pilih kelas, upload file (PDF/PPT/Video)
207: - Validasi tipe file & ukuran (max sesuai konfigurasi server)
208: - Daftar materi yang sudah diupload (bisa edit/hapus)
209: 
210: #### 3. Kelola Tugas
211: 
212: - Form buat tugas: judul, deskripsi, pilih kelas, deadline (date-time picker)
213: - Daftar tugas: tampilkan judul, kelas, deadline, jumlah yang sudah kumpul
214: - Tombol: Edit, Hapus tugas
215: 
216: #### 4. Input Nilai
217: 
218: - Pilih tugas dari dropdown
219: - Tampilkan tabel: nama siswa, status pengumpulan, file, kolom input nilai
220: - Submit nilai -> update tabel pengumpulan_tugas (nilai, status='dinilai')
221: 
222: #### 5. Absensi Online
223: 
224: - Pilih kelas & tanggal
225: - Cek: apakah sesi absensi sudah dibuat hari ini (query ke tabel absensi)
226: - Jika belum: buat sesi baru, tampilkan daftar siswa dengan toggle status
227: - Status: Hadir / Izin / Sakit / Alfa (radio button per siswa)
228: - Submit -> simpan ke absensi_detail
229: 
230: #### 6. Laporan (Guru)
231: 
232: - Filter: pilih kelas
233: - Rekap nilai siswa per tugas
234: - Rekap absensi siswa per bulan
235: - Grafik sederhana: persentase kehadiran
236: 
237: ### [D] SISWA
238: 
239: #### 1. Dashboard Siswa
240: 
241: - Daftar materi terbaru dari kelas siswa
242: - Daftar tugas aktif (belum dikumpulkan, belum deadline)
243: - Nilai terkini yang sudah diinput guru
244: 
245: #### 2. Lihat Materi
246: 
247: - Daftar materi sesuai kelas siswa (filter per mata pelajaran opsional)
248: - Tombol: Download / Lihat Preview
249: 
250: #### 3. Kumpul Tugas
251: 
252: - Daftar tugas yang harus dikumpulkan (beserta deadline & status)
253: - Klik tugas -> form upload jawaban (file PDF/Word/ZIP)
254: - Validasi: hanya bisa kumpul sebelum deadline
255: - Status berubah jadi 'dikumpulkan'
256: 
257: #### 4. Lihat Nilai
258: 
259: - Tabel: nama tugas, tanggal kumpul, nilai, status
260: - Jika belum dinilai: tampilkan "-"
261: 
262: ---
263: 
264: ## BAGIAN 4 : ALUR LOGIKA UTAMA (PSEUDOCODE)
265: 
266: ### [1] Proses Login
267: 
268: ```
269: START
270:   Buka halaman login
271:   Input email & password
272:   IF email kosong OR password kosong THEN
273:     Tampilkan error "Field tidak boleh kosong"
274:   ELSE
275:     Query: SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = input_email
276:     IF user tidak ditemukan THEN
277:       Tampilkan error "Email tidak terdaftar"
278:     ELSE
279:       Verifikasi password_hash(input_password) == users.password
280:       IF tidak cocok THEN
281:         Tampilkan error "Password salah"
282:       ELSE
283:         Set $_SESSION['user_id'] = users.id
284:         Set $_SESSION['nama']    = users.nama
285:         Set $_SESSION['role']    = users.role
286:         IF role == 'admin'  THEN redirect ke /pages/admin/dashboard.php
287:         IF role == 'guru'   THEN redirect ke /pages/guru/dashboard.php
288:         IF role == 'siswa'  THEN redirect ke /pages/siswa/dashboard.php
289:       END IF
290:     END IF
291:   END IF
292: END
293: ```
294: 
295: ### [2] Proses Upload Materi (Guru)
296: 
297: ```
298: START
299:   Guru memilih kelas & mengisi form materi
300:   Klik submit
301:   Validasi: judul tidak kosong, kelas dipilih, file diupload
302:   Cek tipe file: hanya PDF, PPT, PPTX, MP4 yang diizinkan
303:   Cek ukuran file: max 50MB (sesuai php.ini)
304:   IF validasi gagal THEN tampilkan pesan error
305:   ELSE
306:     Generate nama file unik (uniqid + ekstensi asli)
307:     Pindahkan file ke /assets/uploads/materi/
308:     INSERT INTO materi (id_guru, id_kelas, judul, deskripsi, file, tanggal_upload)
309:     Tampilkan pesan sukses
310:   END IF
311: END
312: ```
313: 
314: ### [3] Proses Pengumpulan Tugas (Siswa)
315: 
316: ```
317: START
318:   Siswa membuka halaman tugas
319:   Sistem query tugas berdasarkan id_kelas siswa
320:   Siswa memilih tugas & upload file jawaban
321:   Validasi: file tidak kosong, deadline belum lewat
322:   IF deadline sudah lewat THEN
323:     Tampilkan "Batas waktu pengumpulan telah habis"
324:   ELSE IF file tidak valid THEN
325:     Tampilkan pesan error format file
326:   ELSE
327:     Generate nama file unik
328:     Pindahkan ke /assets/uploads/tugas/
329:     Cek apakah sudah pernah mengumpulkan (id_tugas + id_siswa)
330:     IF sudah ada THEN UPDATE (replace file lama)
331:     ELSE INSERT INTO pengumpulan_tugas (id_tugas, id_siswa, file, status, waktu_kumpul)
332:     Tampilkan pesan sukses
333:   END IF
334: END
335: ```
336: 
337: ### [4] Proses Absensi (Guru)
338: 
339: ```
340: START
341:   Guru memilih kelas & tanggal
342:   Query: SELECT * FROM absensi WHERE id_kelas = X AND tanggal = Y
343:   IF sudah ada sesi THEN
344:     Load data absensi_detail yang sudah ada (mode edit)
345:   ELSE
346:     INSERT INTO absensi (id_kelas, id_guru, tanggal)
347:     Ambil id_absensi baru
348:     Query siswa di kelas: SELECT id_siswa FROM kelas_siswa WHERE id_kelas = X
349:     Untuk setiap siswa: INSERT INTO absensi_detail (id_absensi, id_siswa, status='alfa')
350:   END IF
351:   Tampilkan form daftar siswa dengan status toggle (Hadir/Izin/Sakit/Alfa)
352:   Guru submit form
353:   UPDATE absensi_detail SET status = input_status WHERE id_detail = X
354:   Tampilkan pesan sukses
355: END
356: ```
357:

503: ---
504: 
505: ## BAGIAN 9 : PANDUAN SESSION & KEAMANAN DASAR
506: 
507: Setiap halaman yang memerlukan login wajib menyertakan:
508: 
509: ```php
510: <?php
511: session_start();
512: if (!isset($_SESSION['user_id'])) {
513:     header("Location: /auth/login.php");
514:     exit;
515: }
516: // Cek role untuk halaman tertentu:
517: if ($_SESSION['role'] !== 'admin') {
518:     header("Location: /auth/login.php");
519:     exit;
520: }
521: ?>
522: ```
523: 
524: ### Aturan Keamanan
525: 
526: | No | Aturan |
527: |----|--------|
528: | 1 | Password disimpan dengan `password_hash($pass, PASSWORD_BCRYPT)` |
529: | 2 | Verifikasi dengan `password_verify($input, $hash)` |
530: | 3 | Gunakan prepared statement (PDO) untuk semua query |
531: | 4 | Validasi & sanitasi semua input sebelum diproses |
532: | 5 | Cek role di setiap halaman sesuai hak akses |
533: | 6 | Nama file upload di-rename menggunakan `uniqid()` untuk menghindari overwrite |
534: 
535: ---
536: 
537: ## BAGIAN 10 : CONTOH KONEKSI DATABASE (config/database.php)
538: 
539: ```php
540: <?php
541: $host     = 'localhost';
542: $dbname   = 'simp_web';
543: $username = 'root';
544: $password = '';
545: 
546: try {
547:     $pdo = new PDO(
548:         "mysql:host=$host;dbname=$dbname;charset=utf8mb4",
549:         $username,
550:         $password,
551:         [
552:             PDO::ATTR_ERRMODE            => PDO::ERRMODE_EXCEPTION,
553:             PDO::ATTR_DEFAULT_FETCH_MODE => PDO::FETCH_ASSOC,
554:         ]
555:     );
556: } catch (PDOException $e) {
557:     die("Koneksi gagal: " . $e->getMessage());
558: }
559: ?>
560: ```

109: 
110: ## Brand & Style
111: 
112: The design system is engineered for a high-performance Learning Management System (LMS) specifically tailored for SMA/SMK environments. The brand personality is **Professional, Systematic, and Trustworthy**, prioritizing clarity and ease of navigation for three distinct user archetypes: Admins, Teachers, and Students.
113: 
114: The visual style is **Corporate Modern**, characterized by:
115: - **High Information Density:** Clean layouts that allow for complex data (grades, schedules, curricula) to be scanned quickly.
116: - **Structural Integrity:** Use of rigid alignment and consistent spacing to evoke a sense of institutional reliability.
117: - **Minimalist Aesthetic:** Stripping away decorative elements like gradients or complex illustrations to focus purely on educational content.
118: - **Functional Clarity:** Ensuring that the UI feels mature and sophisticated, intentionally avoiding "gamified" or "childish" tropes often found in primary education software.
119: 
120: ## Colors
121: 
122: The palette is anchored by a high-trust **Primary Blue**, used specifically for actionable items and brand identifiers. 
123: 
124: - **Primary (#1A73E8):** Used for primary buttons, active states, and focus indicators.
125: - **Neutral Surface (#F5F6FA):** Applied to card backgrounds, sidebars, and secondary layout containers to create subtle separation from the white page background.
126: - **Typography Primary (#202124):** High-contrast dark gray for maximum legibility in body text and headings.
127: - **Typography Secondary (#5F6368):** Medium gray for labels, hints, and meta-data.
128: - **Semantic Colors:** Green and Red are reserved for grading status, submission success, or error alerts, following the standard professional utility scale.
129: 
130: ## Typography
131: 
132: This design system utilizes **Inter** as the sole typeface family to ensure a clean, systematic feel across all platforms. The scale is built on a 14px base for standard body content, optimized for data-heavy portals.
133: 
134: - **Headlines:** Use semi-bold weights with slight negative letter-spacing to appear compact and authoritative.
135: - **Body Text:** Standardized at 14px (`body-md`) for dashboards and 16px (`body-lg`) for long-form reading materials or lesson content.
136: - **Labels:** Used for table headers, small captions, and tag text. These are slightly tighter and use a medium weight for clarity.
137: - **Monospaced:** JetBrains Mono is suggested for any technical SMK subjects involving programming or technical data.
138: 
139: ## Layout & Spacing
140: 
141: The layout follows a **Fixed Grid** philosophy for desktop dashboards to ensure consistent information density, while transitioning to a **Fluid Grid** for mobile views.
142: 
143: - **The 8px Grid:** All internal spacing (padding, margins between elements) must be multiples of 4px/8px to maintain mathematical harmony.
144: - **Desktop:** 12-column grid with 24px gutters. The main navigation sidebar is fixed at 256px, while the content area expands to a maximum of 1440px.
145: - **Tablet:** 8-column grid with 20px gutters. Sidebars usually collapse into a hamburger menu or narrow icon bar.
146: - **Mobile:** 4-column fluid grid with 16px outer margins. Vertical stacking is mandatory for all card-based content.
147: 
148: ## Elevation & Depth
149: 
150: To maintain a professional and flat aesthetic, depth is communicated through **Tonal Layers** and a single, disciplined shadow style.
151: 
152: - **Base Layer:** The white (#FFFFFF) background represents the lowest level.
153: - **Surface Layer:** The light gray (#F5F6FA) is used for "Well" areas or section containers that house multiple cards.
154: - **Card Elevation:** High-priority content containers use a white background with a specific "Soft Shadow": `0 2px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08)`. This provides just enough lift to separate content without appearing heavy.
155: - **Interactive States:** On hover, cards may increase shadow spread slightly (`0 4px 12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12)`) to indicate clickability.
156: - **Borders:** 1px solid borders in #E0E0E0 are used for input fields and table rows instead of shadows to keep the UI crisp.
157: 
158: ## Shapes
159: 
160: The design system utilizes **Soft** roundedness to balance professional rigor with modern approachability.
161: 
162: - **Standard Elements (0.25rem / 4px):** Applied to buttons, input fields, and small tags. This "sharp-soft" look maintains a serious, academic tone.
163: - **Large Elements (0.5rem / 8px):** Applied to cards, modals, and featured image containers.
164: - **Full Rounded:** Only used for "Pill" tags (e.g., status indicators like "Completed" or "Pending") and user avatars.
165: 
166: ## Components
167: 
168: - **Buttons:** Primary buttons use the Primary Blue with white text. Secondary buttons use a transparent background with a #E0E0E0 border and #202124 text. No gradients allowed.
169: - **Input Fields:** 1px solid border (#E0E0E0). On focus, the border changes to Primary Blue with a 2px thickness. Labels are always visible above the field in `label-sm`.
170: - **Cards:** White background, 8px corner radius, and the standard 0 2px 8px shadow. Used for course modules, student profiles, and grade reports.
171: - **Chips/Status:** Small height (24px or 32px), pill-shaped. Background colors should be very desaturated (e.g., light green for "Passed") with high-contrast dark text.
172: - **Lists/Tables:** Use alternating row colors (White and #F5F6FA) or simple 1px dividers. Table headers must be in `label-sm` with a light gray background.
173: - **Navigation:** Vertical sidebar for desktop with icons (24px) paired with `body-md` text. Active state indicated by a 4px vertical bar on the left edge in Primary Blue.
174: - **LMS Specifics:**
175:     - *Grade Indicator:* A dedicated circular or box-shaped badge with a bold weight for the score.
176:     - *Timeline/Progress Bar:* A simple 4px thick horizontal track using #F5F6FA with a Primary Blue fill indicating completion percentage.

(End of file - total 176 lines)

3. Create `config/app.php` (constants like BASE_URL, ROLE_ constants, etc.)

- Role constants

- Allowed file types

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "D:\\rpl\\code\\simp-web\\sql\\simp_web.sql",
  "content": "-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Database: simp_web\n-- Sistem Informasi Manajemen Pembelajaran Berbasis Web\n-- SMA/SMK — Admin, Guru, Siswa\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n\nCREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS simp_web CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\nUSE simp_web;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: users\n-- Menyimpan akun Admin, Guru, dan Siswa\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    id          INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    nama        VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    email       VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,\n    password    VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n    role        ENUM('admin','guru','siswa') NOT NULL,\n    created_at  TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: kelas\n-- Data kelas dengan wali kelas (referensi ke users role=guru)\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE kelas (\n    id_kelas    INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    nama_kelas  VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,\n    wali_kelas  INT,\n    FOREIGN KEY (wali_kelas) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: kelas_siswa\n-- Relasi many-to-many antara siswa dan kelas\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE kelas_siswa (\n    id          INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    id_kelas    INT NOT NULL,\n    id_siswa    INT NOT NULL,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_siswa) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    UNIQUE KEY unique_siswa_kelas (id_kelas, id_siswa)\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: materi\n-- File materi yang diupload oleh Guru\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE materi (\n    id_materi       INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    id_guru         INT NOT NULL,\n    id_kelas        INT NOT NULL,\n    judul           VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,\n    deskripsi       TEXT,\n    file            VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n    tanggal_upload  DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_guru)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: tugas\n-- Tugas yang dibuat oleh Guru dengan deadline\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE tugas (\n    id_tugas    INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    id_guru     INT NOT NULL,\n    id_kelas    INT NOT NULL,\n    judul       VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,\n    deskripsi   TEXT,\n    deadline    DATETIME NOT NULL,\n    created_at  TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_guru)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: pengumpulan_tugas\n-- Jawaban tugas yang dikumpulkan siswa + nilai dari guru\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE pengumpulan_tugas (\n    id_pengumpulan  INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    id_tugas        INT NOT NULL,\n    id_siswa        INT NOT NULL,\n    file            VARCHAR(255),\n    nilai           FLOAT DEFAULT NULL,\n    status          ENUM('belum','dikumpulkan','dinilai') DEFAULT 'belum',\n    waktu_kumpul    DATETIME,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_tugas)  REFERENCES tugas(id_tugas) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_siswa)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    UNIQUE KEY unique_tugas_siswa (id_tugas, id_siswa)\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: absensi\n-- Sesi absensi per kelas per tanggal\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE absensi (\n    id_absensi  INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    id_kelas    INT NOT NULL,\n    id_guru     INT NOT NULL,\n    tanggal     DATE NOT NULL,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_kelas) REFERENCES kelas(id_kelas) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_guru)  REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    UNIQUE KEY unique_kelas_tanggal (id_kelas, tanggal)\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Tabel: absensi_detail\n-- Status kehadiran setiap siswa dalam sesi absensi\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nCREATE TABLE absensi_detail (\n    id_detail   INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,\n    id_absensi  INT NOT NULL,\n    id_siswa    INT NOT NULL,\n    status      ENUM('hadir','izin','sakit','alfa') DEFAULT 'alfa',\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_absensi) REFERENCES absensi(id_absensi) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    FOREIGN KEY (id_siswa)   REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    UNIQUE KEY unique_absensi_siswa (id_absensi, id_siswa)\n) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\n\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\n-- Seed Data: Akun Admin Default\n-- Password: admin123 (bcrypt hash)\n-- --------------------------------------------------------\nINSERT INTO users (nama, email, password, role) VALUES\n('Administrator', 'admin@simp.web', 2. `auth/logout.php` - Simple logout script

The login page from the mockup uses:
- Tailwind CSS CDN with specific Academic Precision colors
- Inter font
- Material Symbols Outlined
- Split background gradient
- Custom shadow
- Password visibility toggle

I need to make this a PHP file that:
- Shows the login form (from the mockup)
- Processes form submission
- Validates credentials against database
- Sets session variables
- Redirects based on role

Let me create both files now.

---

## Assistant (Build · Big Pickle · 22.9s)

_Thinking:_

Now I have a clear picture of all three layouts:

1. **Admin Dashboard** - has a TopAppBar with name/role + sidebar with nav items (Dashboard, Kelola Kelas, Kelola Akun, Laporan, Logout) + main content area

2. **Teacher Dashboard** - same TopAppBar + sidebar (Dashboard, Materi, Tugas, Presensi, Nilai, Laporan)

3. **Student Dashboard** - same TopAppBar + sidebar (Dashboard, Materi, Tugas, Laporan Nilai)

The common patterns:
- Fixed TopAppBar with `h-16`, `bg-surface`, `border-b border-outline-variant`
- Fixed sidebar `w-64`, hidden on mobile, `bg-surface`, `border-r border-outline-variant`
- Main content with `md:ml-64`, `pt-20` (or `pt-24`)
- Bottom nav bar on mobile (`md:hidden`)
- All use `soft-shadow` (0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.08))

392:                 tabButtons.forEach(b => {

396:                     if(icon) icon.remove();

399:                 btn.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant');

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "D:\\rpl\\code\\simp-web\\pages\\admin\\kelola_kelas.php",
  "content": "<?php\n$title = 'Kelola Kelas';\n$currentPage = 'kelas';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../includes/header.php';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../config/database.php';\n\n$message = '';\n$messageType = '';\n\nif ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST') {\n    $action = $_POST['action'] ?? '';\n\n    if ($action === 'tambah') {\n        $namaKelas  = trim($_POST['nama_kelas'] ?? '');\n        $waliKelas  = $_POST['wali_kelas'] ?? '';\n        if ($namaKelas === '') {\n            $message = 'Nama kelas harus diisi.';\n            $messageType = 'error';\n        } else {\n            $stmt = $pdo->prepare(\"INSERT INTO kelas (nama_kelas, wali_kelas) VALUES (?, ?)\");\n            $stmt->execute([$namaKelas, $waliKelas ?: null]);\n            $idKelas = $pdo->lastInsertId();\n            if (!empty($_POST['siswa'])) {\n                $stmtSiswa = $pdo->prepare(\"INSERT INTO kelas_siswa (id_kelas, id_siswa) VALUES (?, ?)\");\n                foreach ($_POST['siswa'] as $idSiswa) {\n                    $stmtSiswa->execute([$idKelas, $idSiswa]);\n                }\n            }\n            $message = 'Kelas berhasil ditambahkan.';\n            $messageType = 'success';\n        }\n    } elseif ($action === 'edit') {\n        $idKelas   = $_POST['id_kelas'] ?? 0;\n        $namaKelas = trim($_POST['nama_kelas'] ?? '');\n        $waliKelas = $_POST['wali_kelas'] ?? '';\n        if ($namaKelas === '') {\n            $message = 'Nama kelas harus diisi.';\n            $messageType = 'error';\n        } else {\n            $stmt = $pdo->prepare(\"UPDATE kelas SET nama_kelas = ?, wali_kelas = ? WHERE id_kelas = ?\");\n            $stmt->execute([$namaKelas, $waliKelas ?: null, $idKelas]);\n            $pdo->prepare(\"DELETE FROM kelas_siswa WHERE id_kelas = ?\")->execute([$idKelas]);\n            if (!empty($_POST['siswa'])) {\n                $stmtSiswa = $pdo->prepare(\"INSERT INTO kelas_siswa (id_kelas, id_siswa) VALUES (?, ?)\");\n                foreach ($_POST['siswa'] as $idSiswa) {\n                    $stmtSiswa->execute([$idKelas, $idSiswa]);\n                }\n            }\n            $message = 'Kelas berhasil diperbarui.';\n            $messageType = 'success';\n        }\n    } elseif ($action === 'hapus') {\n        $idKelas = $_POST['id_kelas'] ?? 0;\n        $pdo->prepare(\"DELETE FROM kelas WHERE id_kelas = ?\")->execute([$idKelas]);\n        $message = 'Kelas berhasil dihapus.';\n        $messageType = 'success';\n    }\n}\n\n$kelasList = $pdo->query(\"\n    SELECT k.*, u.nama as wali_nama,\n        (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM kelas_siswa ks WHERE ks.id_kelas = k.id_kelas) as jumlah_siswa\n    FROM kelas k\n    LEFT JOIN users u ON k.wali_kelas = u.id\n    ORDER BY k.nama_kelas\n\")->fetchAll();\n\n$guruList = $pdo->query(\"SELECT id, nama FROM users WHERE role='guru' ORDER BY nama\")->fetchAll();\n$siswaList = $pdo->query(\"SELECT id, nama FROM users WHERE role='siswa' ORDER BY nama\")->fetchAll();\n\n$siswaPerKelas = [];\nif (!empty($kelasList)) {\n    $ids = array_column($kelasList, 'id_kelas');\n    $placeholders = implode(',', array_fill(0, count($ids), '?'));\n    $stmt = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT id_kelas, id_siswa FROM kelas_siswa WHERE id_kelas IN ($placeholders)\");\n    $stmt->execute($ids);\n    foreach ($stmt->fetchAll() as $row) {\n        $siswaPerKelas[$row['id_kelas']][] = $row['id_siswa'];\n    }\n}\n?>\n<div class=\"max-w-[1440px] mx-auto\">\n    <?php if ($message): ?>\n        <div class=\"mb-6 px-4 py-3 rounded-lg flex items-center gap-2 border <?= $messageType === 'error' ? document.getElementById('modalUserTitle').textContent = 'Edit Pengguna';\n    document.getElementById('editId').value = id;\n    document.getElementById('formNama').value = nama;\n document.getElementById('passLabel').textContent = '(kosongkan jika tidak diganti)';\n    document.getElementById('formPassword').required = false;\n document.querySelectorAll('#userTable tbody tr').forEach(row => {\n        if (row.dataset.nama && row.dataset.email) {\n            row.style.display = row.dataset.nama.includes(q) || row.dataset.email.includes(q) ? '' : 'none';\n        }\n    });\n}\n</script>\n<?php require_once __DIR__ . '/../../includes/footer.php'; ?>\n"

397:         // Micro-interaction for Drag and Drop area
398:         const dropZone = document.querySelector('.group.cursor-pointer');
399:         const fileInput = document.querySelector('input[type="file"]');
400: 
401:         dropZone.addEventListener('click', () => fileInput.click());
402: 
403:         dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
404:             e.preventDefault();
405:             dropZone.classList.add('border-primary', 'bg-primary-container/10');
406:         });
407: 
408:         dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
409:             dropZone.classList.remove('border-primary', 'bg-primary-container/10');
410:         });
411: 
412:         dropZone.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
413:             e.preventDefault();
414:             dropZone.classList.remove('border-primary', 'bg-primary-container/10');
415:             const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
416:             if (files.length > 0) {
417:                 alert(`${files.length} file(s) siap diunggah.`);
418:             }
419:         });
420: 
421:         // Simpan Materi Button Animation
422:         const saveBtn = document.querySelector('button.bg-primary');
423:         saveBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
424:             this.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined animate-spin text-[18px]">progress_activity</span> Menyimpan...';
425:             setTimeout(() => {
426:                 this.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined text-[18px]">check_circle</span> Berhasil';
427:                 setTimeout(() => {
428:                     this.innerHTML = '<span class="material-symbols-outlined text-[18px]">save</span> Simpan Materi';
429:                 }, 2000);
430:             }, 1500);
431:         });
432:     </script>
433: </body></html>

(End of file - total 433 lines)
</content>

{
  "content": "<?php\n$title = 'Laporan';\n$currentPage = 'laporan';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../includes/header.php';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../config/database.php';\n\n$idGuru = $_SESSION['user_id'];\n\n// Get teacher's classes\n$kelasList = $pdo->prepare(\"\n    SELECT DISTINCT k.* FROM kelas k\n    JOIN tugas t ON t.id_kelas = k.id_kelas\n    WHERE t.id_guru = ?\n    ORDER BY k.nama_kelas\n\");\n$kelasList->execute([$idGuru]);\n$kelasList = $kelasList->fetchAll();\n\n$selectedKelas = $_GET['id_kelas'] ?? 0;\n$selectedTugas = $_GET['id_tugas'] ?? 0;\n$view = $_GET['view'] ?? 'nilai';\n\n$tugasList = [];\nif ($selectedKelas) {\n    $tl = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT * FROM tugas WHERE id_guru = ? AND id_kelas = ? ORDER BY created_at DESC\");\n    $tl->execute([$idGuru, $selectedKelas]);\n    $tugasList = $tl->fetchAll();\n}\n\n// Statistik per kelas\n$statsKelas = [];\nforeach ($kelasList as $k) {\n    $s = $pdo->prepare(\"\n        SELECT\n            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM kelas_siswa WHERE id_kelas = ?) as total_siswa,\n            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM tugas WHERE id_kelas = ? AND id_guru = ?) as total_tugas,\n            (SELECT ROUND(AVG(pt.nilai), 1) FROM pengumpulan_tugas pt JOIN tugas t ON pt.id_tugas = t.id_tugas WHERE t.id_kelas = ? AND t.id_guru = ? AND pt.nilai IS NOT NULL) as rata_nilai\n    \");\n    $s->execute([$k['id_kelas'], $k['id_kelas'], $idGuru, $k['id_kelas'], $idGuru]);\n    $statsKelas[$k['id_kelas']] = $s->fetch();\n}\n\n// Detail nilai per tugas\n$detailNilai = [];\nif ($selectedTugas) {\n    $dn = $pdo->prepare(\"\n        SELECT u.nama as nama_siswa, pt.status, pt.nilai, pt.catatan_guru, pt.tanggal_kumpul\n        FROM pengumpulan_tugas pt\n        JOIN users u ON pt.id_siswa = u.id_user\n        JOIN kelas_siswa ks ON ks.id_siswa = u.id_user\n        WHERE pt.id_tugas = ? ## Assistant (Build · Big Pickle · 71.6s)

_Thinking:_

Now I have all the context I need. Let me create all 4 student pages.

Key information:
- Student's class is determined from `kelas_siswa` table
- `UPLOAD_PATH_TUGAS` is the upload directory for assignments
- `ALLOWED_FILE_TYPES_TUGAS` are: pdf, doc, docx, zip, rar, jpg, jpeg, png
- `MAX_FILE_SIZE` is 50MB
- `pengumpulan_tugas` table has: id_pengumpulan, id_tugas, id_siswa, file, status (belum/dikumpulkan/dinilai/terlambat), nilai, catatan_guru, tanggal_kumpul
- `tugas` table has: id_tugas, id_guru, id_kelas, judul, deskripsi, deadline, created_at
- `materi` table has: id_materi, id_guru, id_kelas, judul, deskripsi, file, tanggal_upload

Let me create all 4 files now.

1. dashboard.php — stats + recent materials + active tasks + recent grades
2. lihat_materi.php — materials by class, download
3. kumpul_tugas.php — list active tasks with upload form
4. lihat_nilai.php — grade table

I also need to handle the case where a student doesn't have a class assigned yet.

Let me write all 4 files in parallel.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "<?php\n$title = 'Dashboard Siswa';\n$currentPage = 'dashboard';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../includes/header.php';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../config/database.php';\n\n$idSiswa = $_SESSION['user_id'];\n\n// Get student's class\n$kelasSiswa = $pdo->prepare(\"\n    SELECT k.id_kelas, k.nama_kelas FROM kelas_siswa ks\n    JOIN kelas k ON ks.id_kelas = k.id_kelas\n    WHERE ks.id_siswa = ?\n\");\n$kelasSiswa->execute([$idSiswa]);\n$kelasSiswa = $kelasSiswa->fetch();\n\n// Stats\n$totalMateri = 0; $totalTugas = 0; $sudahKumpul = 0; $rataNilai = 0;\nif ($kelasSiswa) {\n    $idKelas = $kelasSiswa['id_kelas'];\n\n    $totalMateri = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM materi WHERE id_kelas = ?\");\n    $totalMateri->execute([$idKelas]);\n    $totalMateri = $totalMateri->fetchColumn();\n\n    $totalTugas = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM tugas WHERE id_kelas = ?\");\n    $totalTugas->execute([$idKelas]);\n    $totalTugas = $totalTugas->fetchColumn();\n\n    $sudahKumpul = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_siswa = ? AND status != 'belum'\");\n    $sudahKumpul->execute([$idSiswa]);\n    $sudahKumpul = $sudahKumpul->fetchColumn();\n\n    $rataNilai = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT AVG(nilai) FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_siswa = ? AND nilai IS NOT NULL\");\n    $rataNilai->execute([$idSiswa]);\n    $rataNilai = number_format($rataNilai->fetchColumn() ?: 0, 1);\n}\n\n// Recent materials\n$recentMateri = [];\nif ($kelasSiswa) {\n    $rm = $pdo->prepare(\"\n        SELECT m.*, u.nama as nama_guru FROM materi m\n        JOIN users u ON m.id_guru = u.id_user\n        WHERE m.id_kelas = ? ORDER BY m.tanggal_upload DESC LIMIT 4\n    \");\n    $rm->execute([$kelasSiswa['id_kelas']]);\n    $recentMateri = $rm->fetchAll();\n}\n\n// Active tasks (not past deadline)\n$activeTugas = [];\nif ($kelasSiswa) {\n    $at = $pdo->prepare(\"\n        SELECT t.*, u.nama as nama_guru,\n            (SELECT status FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = t.id_tugas AND id_siswa = ?) as status_saya\n        FROM tugas t\n        JOIN users u ON t.id_guru = u.id_user\n        WHERE t.id_kelas = ? AND t.deadline > NOW()\n        ORDER BY t.deadline ASC LIMIT 4\n    \");\n    $at->execute([$idSiswa, $kelasSiswa['id_kelas']]);\n    $activeTugas = $at->fetchAll();\n}\n\n// Latest grades\n$nilaiTerbaru = [];\nif ($kelasSiswa) {\n    $nt = $pdo->prepare(\"\n        SELECT pt.*, t.judul as judul_tugas FROM pengumpulan_tugas pt\n        JOIN tugas t ON pt.id_tugas = t.id_tugas\n        WHERE pt.id_siswa = ? AND pt.nilai IS NOT NULL\n        ORDER BY pt.tanggal_kumpul DESC LIMIT 4\n    \");\n    $nt->execute([$idSiswa]);\n    $nilaiTerbaru = $nt->fetchAll();\n}\n?>\n<div class=\"max-w-[1440px] mx-auto space-y-8\">\n    <div>\n        <h2 class=\"font-display-lg text-display-lg text-on-surface\">Halo, <?= htmlspecialchars($_SESSION['nama']) ?>!</h2>\n        <p class=\"text-on-surface-variant\">\n            <?php if ($kelasSiswa): ?>\n                Kelas <?= htmlspecialchars($kelasSiswa['nama_kelas']) ?> — Pantau materi, tugas, dan nilai kamu.\n            <?php else: ?>\n                Kamu belum terdaftar di kelas mana pun. Hubungi admin.\n            <?php endif; ?>\n        </p>\n    </div>\n\n    <?php if ($kelasSiswa): ?>\n    <!-- Stats -->\n    <div class=\"grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-gutter\">\n rounded-full bg-primary-container flex items-center justify-center text-primary\"><span class=\"material-symbols-outlined\">book</span></div>\n                <div><p class=\"font-label-sm text-on-surface-variant\">Materi</p><p class=\"text-[28px] font-bold\"><?= $totalMateri ?></p></div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"bg-surface-container-lowest p-6 font-bold\"><?= $sudahKumpul ?>/<?= $totalTugas ?></p></div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"bg-surface-container-lowest p-6 rounded-xl soft-shadow border {
  "content": "<?php\n$title = 'Kumpul Tugas';\n$currentPage = 'tugas';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../includes/header.php';\nrequire_once __DIR__ . '/../../config/database.php';\n\n$idSiswa = $_SESSION['user_id'];\n$message = ''; $messageType = '';\n\n// Get student's class\n$kelasSiswa = $pdo->prepare(\"\n    SELECT k.id_kelas, k.nama_kelas FROM kelas_siswa ks\n    JOIN kelas k ON ks.id_kelas = k.id_kelas\n    WHERE ks.id_siswa = ?\n\");\n$kelasSiswa->execute([$idSiswa]);\n$kelasSiswa = $kelasSiswa->fetch();\n\n// Handle upload\nif ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['kumpul'])) {\n    $idTugas = $_POST['id_tugas'] ?? 0;\n    $file = $_FILES['file'] ?? null;\n\n    // Verify tugas exists and belongs to student's class\n    $cek = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT * FROM tugas WHERE id_tugas = ? AND id_kelas = ? AND deadline > NOW()\");\n    $cek->execute([$idTugas, $kelasSiswa['id_kelas'] ?? 0]);\n    $tugas = $cek->fetch();\n\n    if (!$tugas) {\n        $message = 'Tugas tidak valid atau sudah melewati deadline.';\n        $messageType = 'error';\n    } elseif (!$file || $file['error'] !== UPLOAD_ERR_OK) {\n        $message = 'Pilih file untuk dikumpulkan.';\n        $messageType = 'error';\n    } else {\n        $ext = strtolower(pathinfo($file['name'], PATHINFO_EXTENSION));\n        if (!in_array($ext, ALLOWED_FILE_TYPES_TUGAS)) {\n            $message = 'Tipe file tidak diizinkan.';\n            $messageType = 'error';\n        } elseif ($file['size'] > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {\n            $message = 'Ukuran file maksimal 50MB.';\n            $messageType = 'error';\n        } else {\n            $fileName = uniqid('tugas_') . '.' . $ext;\n            $dest = UPLOAD_PATH_TUGAS . $fileName;\n            if (move_uploaded_file($file['tmp_name'], $dest)) {\n                // Check if already submitted\n                $existing = $pdo->prepare(\"SELECT id_pengumpulan, file FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = ? AND id_siswa = ?\");\n                $existing->execute([$idTugas, $idSiswa]);\n                $ex = $existing->fetch();\n\n                if ($ex) {\n                    // Replace\n                    @unlink(UPLOAD_PATH_TUGAS . $ex['file']);\n                    $pdo->prepare(\"UPDATE pengumpulan_tugas SET file = ?, status = 'dikumpulkan', tanggal_kumpul = NOW() WHERE id_pengumpulan = ?\")\n                        ->execute([$fileName, $ex['id_pengumpulan']]);\n                    $message = 'Tugas berhasil diperbarui.';\n                } else {\n                    $pdo->prepare(\"INSERT INTO pengumpulan_tugas (id_tugas, id_siswa, file, status) VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'dikumpulkan')\")\n                        ->execute([$idTugas, $idSiswa, $fileName]);\n                    $message = 'Tugas berhasil dikumpulkan.';\n                }\n                $messageType = 'success';\n            } else {\n                $message = 'Gagal menyimpan file.';\n                $messageType = 'error';\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Get tasks for student's class\n$tugasList = [];\nif ($kelasSiswa) {\n    $tl = $pdo->prepare(\"\n        SELECT t.*, u.nama as nama_guru,\n            (SELECT id_pengumpulan FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = t.id_tugas AND id_siswa = ?) as id_pengumpulan,\n            (SELECT status FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = t.id_tugas AND id_siswa = ?) as status_saya,\n            (SELECT file FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = t.id_tugas AND id_siswa = ?) as file_saya,\n            (SELECT nilai FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = t.id_tugas AND id_siswa = ?) as nilai_saya,\n            (SELECT catatan_guru FROM pengumpulan_tugas WHERE id_tugas = t.id_tugas AND id_siswa = ?) as catatan_saya\n        FROM tugas t\n        JOIN users u ON t.id_guru = u.id_user\n        WHERE t.id_kelas = ?\n        ORDER BY t.deadline DESC\n    \");\n    $tl->execute([$idSiswa, $idSiswa, $idSiswa, $idSiswa, $idSiswa, $kelasSiswa['id_kelas']]);\n    $tugasList = $tl->fetchAll();\n}\n?>\n<div class=\"max-w-[1440px] mx-auto space-y-8\">\n    <?php if ($message): ?>\n        <div class=\"px-4 py-3 rounded-lg flex items-center gap-2 border <?= $messageType === 'error' ? 'bg-error-container border-error text-on-error-container' : 'bg-green-50 border-green-300 text-green-800' ?>\">\n            <span class=\"material-symbols-outlined text-lg\"><?= $messageType === 'error' ? 'error' : 'check_circle' ?></span>\n            <p class=\"font-body-md\"><?= htmlspecialchars($message) ?></p>\n        </div>\n    <?php endif; ?>\n\n    <div>\n        <h2 class=\"font-display-lg      </p>\n    </div>\n\n    <?php if (!$kelasSiswa): ?>\n    <div class=\"flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20 px-4 text-center\">\n        <div class=\"w-20 h-20 mb-4 rounded-full ?>\n        <section class=\"bg-surface-container-lowest rounded-xl soft-shadow border border-outline-variant overflow-hidden\">\n            <div class=\"p-6 border-b border-outline-variant\">\n                 </div>\n                        <div>\n                            <h3 class=\"font-title-sm text-on-surface\"><?= htmlspecialchars($t['judul']) ?></h3>\n                            <p this.initSmoothScroll();\n    },\n\n    /* Sidebar */\n    initSidebar() {\n        window.toggleMobileSidebar = function () {\n            const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');\n document.getElementById(id);\n        if (!el) return;\n        el.classList.remove('hidden');\n        el.classList.add('animate-scale-in');\n        document.body.classList.add('overflow-hidden');\n    },\n\n    closeModal(id) {\n        const el = document.getElementById(id);\n        if (!el) return;\n        el.classList.add('hidden');\n        el.classList.remove('animate-scale-in');\n        document.body.classList.remove('overflow-hidden');\n    },\n\n    /* File Input Label */\n    initFileInputs() {\n        document.querySelectorAll('input[type=\"file\"]').forEach(input => {\n            input.addEventListener('change', function () {\n                const target = this.dataset.labelTarget || this.closest('label')?.querySelector('span');\n                if (target) {\n                    target.textContent = this.files[0]?.name || target.dataset.placeholder || 'Pilih file...';\n                }\n            });\n        });\n    },\n\n    /* Auto-dismiss notifications */\n    initAutoDismiss() {\n        document.querySelectorAll('[data-auto-dismiss]').forEach(el => {\n            const ms = parseInt(el.dataset.autoDismiss) || 5000;\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                el.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s ease, transform 0.3s ease';\n                el.style.opacity = '0';\n                el.style.transform = 'translateY(-8px)';\n if (!el) return;\n        const today = new Date();\n        const options = { weekday: 'long', year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' };\n        el.innerText = today.toLocaleDateString('id-ID', options);\n    },\n\n    /* Smooth scroll */\n    initSmoothScroll() {\n        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^=\"#\"]').forEach(anchor => {\n            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {\n                const href = this.getAttribute('href');\n                if (href === '#') return;\n                const target = document.querySelector(href);\n                if (target) {\n                    e.preventDefault();\n                    target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });\n                }\n            });\n        });\n    },\n\n    /* Format date */\n    formatDate(dateStr, format = 'long') {\n        const date = new Date(dateStr);\n        if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return dateStr;\n        if (format === 'short') {\n            return date.toLocaleDateString('id-ID', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });\n        }\n        return date.toLocaleDateString('id-ID', { weekday: 'long', day: 'numeric', month: 'long', year: 'numeric' });\n    },\n\n    /* Format time remaining */\n    timeRemaining(dateStr) {\n        const now = new Date().getTime();\n        const target = new Date(dateStr).getTime();\n        const diff = target - now;\n\n        if (diff <= 0) return 'Terlewat';\n\n        const days = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));\n        const hours = Math.floor((diff % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));\n\n        if (days > 0) return `${days} hari ${hours} jam`;\n        if (hours > 0) return `${hours} jam`;\n        return 'Kurang dari 1 jam';\n    },\n\n    /* Confirm dialog wrapper */\n    confirm(message = 'Apakah Anda yakin?') {\n        return window.confirm(message);\n    },\n\n    /* Fetch wrapper */\n    async fetch(url, options = {}) {\n        try {\n            const res = await fetch(url, {\n                headers: { 'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest', ...options.headers },\n                ...options\n            });\n            if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);\n            return await res.json();\n        } catch (err) {\n            console.error('SIMP.fetch error:', err);\n            throw err;\n        }\n    },\n\n    /* Toast notification */\n    toast(message, type = 'success', duration = 4000) {\n        const document.getElementById('toast-container');\n        containerEl.appendChild(toast);\n\n        setTimeout(() => {\n            toast.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s ease, transform 0.3s ease';\n
